***рада.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́да</a> (1372)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́да</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rada</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">rât</i> via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">rada</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">rada</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*rēdaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ráda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́ды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́д</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>rada, Rada <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a parliamentary body in a number of Slavic countries</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">feminine singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́д</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rad</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***ради.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ради.html>ра́ди</a> (948)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ради.html>ра́ди</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rádi</span>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ genitive case</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>for the sake of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ради.html>ра́ди</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rádi</b> menjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">for my sake</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ради.html>ра́ди</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>дете́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rádi</b> detéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">for the sake of the children</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3><p>
The word can be used as both preposition, as in </p><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ради.html>ра́ди</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rádi</b> menjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">for my sake</span></div><p>, and postposition, as in </p><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́га</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ради.html>ра́ди</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Bóga <b>rádi</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">for God's sake</span></div><p>. The latter usage tends to be more phrasal.
</p><hr />
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ра́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ди.html>ди</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>Предло́г</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> послелог; неизменяемое <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>Употребля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>. п.

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">radiatio</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радиация.html>радиа́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">radiácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радиация.html>радиа́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радиация.html>радиа́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радиация.html>радиа́ций</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">радиацио́нный</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>radiation (<i>radioactive energy</i>)</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ра<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ди.html>ди</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ак<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ти́в<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>радиоакти́внее, радиоакти́вней.</i>

***радоваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:радоваться.html>ра́доваться</a> (1855)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радовать.html>ра́довать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rádovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радоваться.html>ра́доваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rádovatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обрадоваться.html>обра́доваться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порадоваться.html>пора́доваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rejoice, to be glad, to be happy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:радоваться.html>ра́доваться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rádovatʹsja</b> za kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to rejoice</b> for someone</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радовать.html>ра́довать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rádovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дость</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rádostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́д</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rad</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радостный.html>ра́достный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rádostnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><b>ра́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>дост<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>ра́достнее, ра́достней.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-рад-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-ост-н</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дость</a> (864)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рада.html>ра́д</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rad</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rádostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́достей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>joy, delight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испуг.html>испу́г</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сменяться.html>сменя́ется</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́достью</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ispúg smenjájetsja <b>rádostʹju</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Fear turns to <b>joy</b>.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испуг.html>испу́г</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смениться.html>смени́лся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́достью</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ispúg smenílsja <b>rádostʹju</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Fear turned to <b>joy</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***радужный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:радужный.html>ра́дужный</a> (8090)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радуга.html>ра́дуг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rádug</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радужный.html>ра́дужный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">rádužnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ра́дужнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ра́дужней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rainbow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:радужный.html>ра́дужная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:форель.html>форе́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rádužnaja</b> forɛ́lʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rainbow trout</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:радужный.html>ра́дужная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оболочка.html>оболо́чка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rádužnaja</b> obolóčka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">iris</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>cheerful
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:радужный.html>ра́дужное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:настроение.html>настрое́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>rádužnoje</b> nastrojénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is in very high spirits</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>optimistic, bright, roseate, rosy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:радужный.html>ра́дужные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жды</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rádužnyje</b> nadéždy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">optimistic expectations</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:радужный.html>ра́дужные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ожидание.html>ожида́ния</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:предвкушение.html>предвкуше́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>rádužnyje</b> ožidánija/predvkušénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">rosy anticipations</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́деть</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:представлять.html>представля́ть</a> что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:радужный.html>ра́дужном</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́те</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vídetʹ/predstavljátʹ štó-libo v <b>rádužnom</b> svéte</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have a radiant/glowing picture of something</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>ра́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>дуж<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радуший.html>раду́шие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">radúšije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:радушный.html>раду́шный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">radúšnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)раду́шнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)раду́шней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cordial, kindly, hearty</li>
<li>hospitable</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
